<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 2.02 Results of Operations and Financial
Condition and Item 7.01 Regulation FD Disclosure</font></b></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following information is furnished
pursuant to Item 2.02 &#147;Results of Operations and Financial Condition&#148; and Item
7.01 &#147;Regulation FD Disclosure.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">On
August&nbsp;31, 2004, MortgageIT Holdings, Inc. (&#147;MortgageIT&#148;) issued a press
release announcing its earnings for the three and six months periods ended
June&nbsp;30, 2004. </font>At 10:00
a.m. on September&nbsp;1, 2004, MortgageIT&#146;s Chairman and Chief Executive
Officer Doug W. Naidus will make a presentation of MortgageIT&#146;s earnings for
the three and six months periods ended June&nbsp;30, 2004 on an investor
conference call, which investors can listen to by following the instructions
set forth in the press release attached hereto as <u>Exhibit 99.1</u>.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">MortgageIT is also reporting that b</font>ecause of its reorganization from an
originator/seller to an originator/investor, MortgageIT will apply a different
accounting policy for its loans originated for investment as compared to the
accounting policy that applies to its loans originated for sale.&#160; As a result of this change, MortgageIT
anticipates a negative, non-cash accounting impact to its third quarter pre-tax
earnings of between $2 million and $3 million.&#160;
Also, MortgageIT&#146;s realizable revenues and earnings at the TRS for the
third and fourth quarters of 2004 will be negatively impacted because it will
be self-originating and retaining approximately $2.4 billion of ARM loans for
investment rather than selling those loans to third party investors, and
therefore will not recognize any gain on sale revenue for these loans.&#160; Instead, the value of the ARM loans retained
in its loan investment portfolio will be realized in the form of net interest
income over the life of the loans.&#160; The
net interest income on its investment portfolio will represent the primary
source of income for the dividends that MortgageIT intends to pay to its
shareholders.</p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<body link="blue" vlink="purple">

<div style="font-family:'Times New Roman';">

<p align="right" style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99.1</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:0pt;text-decoration:none;text-shadow:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">MortgageIT
Holdings, Inc. Reports Second Quarter 2004 Financial Results</font></b></font><br><br></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Reports
$3.4 billion in mortgage funding volume, including record $ 1.5 billion in
purchase (non-refinance) mortgage fundings; launches adjustable rate investment
loan portfolio</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">New
York, N.Y., August&nbsp;31, 2004&#151;MortgageIT Holdings, Inc. (NYSE: MHL) today
announced results for the second quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2004.&#160; MortgageIT Holdings (the Company) completed
its reorganization into a real estate investment trust (REIT) and consummated
its initial public offering on August&nbsp;4, 2004.&#160; Results for the quarter and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2004
relate exclusively to the Company&#146;s predecessor, MortgageIT, Inc., a national
mortgage originator that is now wholly owned and operated by the Company as a
taxable REIT subsidiary.&#160; In this
release and going forward, the Company will refer to its taxable REIT
subsidiary as the &#147;TRS.&#148;&#160; The Company
expects that future results of operations will be different from the TRS&#146;s
historical operating results.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt 3.0pc;text-indent:-1.5pc;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the second quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2004, the Company recognized net income of $2.8 million, or $0.15 per diluted share computed on a pro forma basis.&#160; Actual net income per diluted share was $0.58 for the same period.&#160; Earnings per diluted share are presented on both an actual basis and a pro forma basis for comparative purposes to reflect the consummation of our reorganization and initial public offering on August&nbsp;4, 2004.</font></p><p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt 3.0pc;text-indent:-1.5pc;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p><p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt 3.0pc;text-indent:-1.5pc;"><font size="3" face="Times New Ro
man" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Second quarter loan funding volume was $3.4 billion, which included a Company record $1.5 billion in purchase (non-refinance) mortgage loan volume.</font></p><p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt 3.0pc;text-indent:-1.5pc;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p><p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt 3.0pc;text-indent:-1.5pc;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On August&nbsp;4, 2004, the Company completed its initial public offering and raised net proceeds of approximately $163.8 million, after deducting underwriting d
iscounts and commissions and offering expenses, through the issuance of 14.6 million shares at a price to the public of $12.00 per share.</font></p><p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt 3.0pc;text-indent:-1.5pc;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt 3.0pc;text-indent:-1.5pc;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Since completion of the Company&#146;s initial
public offering, it has successfully launched its fully self-originated
investment loan portfolio, with approximately $500 million in high quality ARM
loans as of August&nbsp;31, 2004, with a weighted average coupon, or WAC, of
5.4%, an average FICO score of 731, an average loan-to-value ratio, or LTV, of
74%, and an average loan size of $288,000.</p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt 3.0pc;text-indent:-1.5pc;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt 3.0pc;text-indent:-1.5pc;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company opened four new retail branches during the quarter, which raises its total branch count to 43 (20 retail and 23 wholesale).</font></p><p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt 3.0pc;text-indent:-1.5pc;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p><p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt 3.0pc;text-indent:-1.5pc;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company established Unified Settlement Services, a wholly owned subsidiary t
hat offers title, settlement and appraisal services.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p><p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Doug Naidus, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer, commented, &#147;We are pleased with our second quarter results.&#160; In our second quarter, the last period before our recent initial public offering and reorganization as a REIT, our national mortgage lending subsidiary generated strong loan fundings, including a Company record $1.5 billion in purchase money mortgage (non-refinance) volume.&#160; Continued solid funding volume has enabled us to get off to a good start in building a high quality, fully self-originated investment loan portfolio.&#160; We anticipate that our first loan securitization will be completed by the end of the third quarter and expect to have funded our fully-leveraged, self-originated investment loan portfolio to approximately $2.4 billion by year end.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>


<div style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;text-align:center;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Outlook and Guidance</font></p><p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p><p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt 3.0pc;text-indent:-1.5pc;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company expects to increase its fully-leveraged, self-originated investment loan portfolio to between $850 million and $1.1 billion during the quarter ending September&nbsp;30, 2004, and to approximately $2.4 billion by year end.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt 3.0pc;text-indent:-1.5pc;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company expects to declare its initial dividend in the fourth quarter of 2004, which will represent the distribution of earnings for the period from the Company&#146;s commencement of operations in August&nbsp;2004 through year end.&#160; The Company expects to commence declaration of regular quarterly dividends in the first quarter of 2005.</font></p><p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt 3.0pc;text-indent:-1.5pc;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt 3.0pc;text-indent:-1.5pc;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Loan funding volume amounted to $5.6 billion
for the first six months of 2004, and the Company anticipates third quarter
loan funding volume of $2.75 billion to $3.25 billion.</p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt 3.0pc;text-indent:-1.5pc;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the tables below, the Company presents both actual (GAAP) and pro forma data, which adjusts the historical data to give effect to the reorganization and the consummation of our initial public offering (assuming the reorganization and the initial public offering were each consummated on January&nbsp;1, 2003).&#160; Management believes this pro forma data is useful because the Company had not completed its reorganization into a REIT or its initial public offering during the second quarter, and the issuance of its shares pursuant to these transactions will be reflected in future financial reports.</font></p><p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Conference Call Information</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">MortgageIT Holdings, Inc.
will hold an investor conference call to discuss second quarter financial
performance at 10:00 a.m., Eastern Time, Wednesday, September&nbsp;1,
2004.&#160; Interested parties may listen to
the call by dialing 888-277-8636 (U.S.), or 973-582-2785 (International), or by

available on the Company&#146;s corporate website.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">About MortgageIT Holdings,
Inc.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">MortgageIT Holdings, Inc.
(NYSE: MHL) was formed to act as the holding company of MortgageIT, Inc.
(MortgageIT), its wholly owned residential mortgage lending subsidiary.&#160; MortgageIT is a full-service residential mortgage
banking company that is licensed to originate loans throughout the United
States.&#160; MortgageIT originates
single-family residential mortgage loans of all types, with particular focus on
prime adjustable-rate (ARM) and fixed-rate, first-lien residential mortgage
loans.&#160; MortgageIT Holdings is organized
and conducts its operations to qualify as a real estate investment trust (REIT)
for federal income tax purposes.&#160;
MortgageIT is organized and operates as MortgageIT Holdings&#146; taxable
REIT subsidiary.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pc 0pc .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

loan portfolio, our anticipated loan funding volume and our ability to
successfully complete a securitization transaction. These statements are based
on management&#146;s current expectations and beliefs and are subject to a number of
trends and uncertainties that could cause actual results to differ materially
from those described in the forward-looking statements.&#160; MortgageIT Holdings can give no assurance
that its expectations will be attained. Factors that could cause actual results
to differ materially from MortgageIT Holdings&#146; expectations include, but are
not limited to, MortgageIT&#146;s continued ability to originate new loans,
including loans that we deem suitable for our securitization portfolio; changes
in the capital markets, including changes in interest rates and/or credit
spreads; and other risks detailed in MortgageIT Holdings&#146; Registration
Statement on Form S-11 that was declared effective by the Securities and

esented, assuming that each of the following events had occurred on January&nbsp;1, 2003:&#160; (i) the exchange of all common and preferred shares of MortgageIT (assuming each share of the Company&#146;s common stock was exchanged for approximately 12.80 shares of MortgageIT) pursuant to the reorganization (as described in the Company&#146;s Registration Statement on Form S-11 that was declared effective by the SEC on July&nbsp;29, 2004); and (ii) the Company&#146;s initial public offering.</font></p>
